msg:Three tips for guests who want to stay at this hotel: 1- Open the door and smell carefully to see if there is any smell of smoke. This is especially important for those who are sensitive to smoke. Don't just believe the promotion of a smoke-free hotel and trust your sense of smell. If there is a smell, be sure to ask to change rooms. 2- The quilt provided at a normal room temperature of 22-25 degrees can't cover it at all. It's too thick. Too hot! I slept in a bathrobe. Refer to the picture. 3- The bathroom door must be opened and closed gently. If you close the door casually, you will be startled. See the video. This is my feeling about this five-star hotel. For reference. The hotel swimming pool is good. The water temperature is just right.

name:X‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçt‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçn
info:Executive Room, Executive level, Guest room, 1 King
info:Stayed in September 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:13 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted September 5, 2023
msg:Room facilities:
The executive room is located above the 25th floor. It is very quiet. The room is 40 square meters, which is a bit cramped for an executive room. The room structure is similar to Conrad, and the bathroom sliding door can be opened. The room is very new, modernly decorated, the bathroom quality is good, and the bathtub faucet is awesome. There is a building opposite the window, and there is no view to speak of.

Restaurant:
The breakfast is complete with Chinese and Western styles, rich in variety, and the experience is very good. The scrambled eggs and egg rolls at the egg stall are recommended. The executive lounge has fewer hot dishes for dinner, but the wine and beverage category is sufficient, suitable for friends who like to drink a cup. The executive lounge has very few afternoon tea varieties, only fruit tarts, cookies, and coffee. It is said that there are snacks, but they were not served until I left...

Location and transportation:
This is a disadvantage. It is located in Jinnan, far away from the city, and next to the convention and exhibition center. It will be very convenient to stay for business meetings.

Service:
The service staff has a very good attitude. From the front desk staff to the cleaning staff, to the restaurant staff, they are all polite. This is definitely a leader in the hotel industry in Tianjin. The training is indeed in place. We also gave you fruits and cookies when you checked in, and we also delayed your check-out to 4:00. I heard that the gym and swimming pool are also good, but it's a pity that I didn't bring a swimsuit to experience it.
